## Making a Choropleth
These maps dont have labels because they are used on the poster for this work. Therefore they are saved with intuitive names and in a vector graphics format.


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuYGBgclxuIyBjc2IgbWFwXG5nZ3Bsb3QoKSArXG4gIGdlb21fc2YoZGF0YSA9IGJnKSArXG4gIGdlb21fc2YoZGF0YSA9IG1fYWxsLCBtYXBwaW5nID0gYWVzKGZpbGwgPSBjc2IpKSArXG4gIHRoZW1lKGF4aXMudGV4dCA9IGVsZW1lbnRfYmxhbmsoKSxcbiAgICAgICAgYXhpcy50aWNrcyA9IGVsZW1lbnRfYmxhbmsoKSxcbiAgICAgICAgcGFuZWwuZ3JpZC5tYWpvciA9IGVsZW1lbnRfbGluZShjb2xvciA9IE5BKSxcbiAgICAgICAgcGFuZWwuYmFja2dyb3VuZCA9IGVsZW1lbnRfYmxhbmsoKSxcbiAgICAgICAgcGxvdC5iYWNrZ3JvdW5kID0gZWxlbWVudF9yZWN0KGZpbGwgPSBcXHRyYW5zcGFyZW50XFwsIGNvbG9yID0gTkEpLFxuICAgICAgICBsZWdlbmQuYmFja2dyb3VuZCA9IGVsZW1lbnRfcmVjdChmaWxsID0gXFx0cmFuc3BhcmVudFxcLCBjb2xvciA9IE5BKVxuICAgICAgICApICtcbiAgc2NhbGVfZmlsbF92aXJpZGlzKG5hbWUgPSBcXENTQiBDYWxsc1xcLCBndWlkZSA9IGd1aWRlX2NvbG9yYmFyKHRpY2tzID0gRiksIGRpcmVjdGlvbiA9IC0xKSArXG4gIGZhY2V0X2dyaWQoLiB+IHllYXIpXG5cbmdnc2F2ZShcXC4uL3Jlc3VsdHMvY3NiX3llYXIucGRmXFwsIGRwaSA9IDUwMCwgYmcgPSBcXHRyYW5zcGFyZW50XFwpXG5gYGBcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
```r
# csb map
ggplot() +
  geom_sf(data = bg) +
  geom_sf(data = m_all, mapping = aes(fill = csb)) +
  theme(axis.text = element_blank(),
        axis.ticks = element_blank(),
        panel.grid.major = element_line(color = NA),
        panel.background = element_blank(),
        plot.background = element_rect(fill = \transparent\, color = NA),
        legend.background = element_rect(fill = \transparent\, color = NA)
        ) +
  scale_fill_viridis(name = \CSB Calls\, guide = guide_colorbar(ticks = F), direction = -1) +
  facet_grid(. ~ year)

ggsave(\../results/csb_year.pdf\, dpi = 500, bg = \transparent\)

<!-- rnb-source-end -->
